pkg/kubelet/.\\n\\n### 1. Pod Lifecycle Manager\\nThe pod lifecycle is managed through a layered architecture:\\n\\n**pkg/kubelet/pod_workers.go**: Contains the `podWorkers` struct (implements the `PodWorkers` interface) which coordinates the overall lifecycle of pods. It manages pod state transitions through `PodWorkerSync`, handling updates, termination, and cleanup of pods. The pod workers orchestrate work items and manage pod synchronization across the kubelet.\\n\\n**pkg/kubelet/kubelet_pods.go**: Implements pod synchronization logic with the `SyncPod` function which prepares the node for pod execution, including volume setup, network configuration, and container management.\\n\\n**pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go**: Contains the `kubeGenericRuntimeManager` which implements the `SyncPod` method - the core runtime-level pod synchronization that coordinates with the container runtime to ensure pods match desired state. This manager delegates to the CRI client for actual container operations.\\n\\n### 2. Container Runtime Interface (CRI) Client\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go**: Contains the `remoteRuntimeService` struct which implements gRPC-based communication with container runtimes. The `NewRemoteRuntimeService` factory function creates the CRI client connection that uses the CRI API specification.\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/services.go**: Defines the `RuntimeService` interface (internalapi.RuntimeService) that abstracts the CRI protocol, including methods for pod/container lifecycle operations, image management, and status reporting.\\n\\nThe CRI client is instantiated in `pkg/kubelet/kubelet.go` via `remote.NewRemoteRuntimeService()` and integrated into the kuberuntime manager.\\n\\n### 3. Volume Manager  \\n**pkg/kubelet/volumemanager/volume_manager.go**: Implements the `VolumeManager` interface through the concrete `volumeManager` struct. This component runs asynchronous loops that track which volumes need to be attached/mounted/unmounted/detached based on pod requirements. It coordinates with the volume populator and reconciler to manage the desired vs. actual state of volumes on the node.\\n\\n### 4. Device Plugin Manager\\nTwo interrelated components handle device management:\\n\\n**pkg/kubelet/pluginmanager/plugin_manager.go**: The general `PluginManager` interface implemented by `pluginManager` struct. This manages generic plugin lifecycle (registration/deregistration) and serves as a framework for various plugin types including device plugins. It uses a desired/actual state of world pattern with a plugin watcher and reconciler.\\n\\n**pkg/kubelet/cm/devicemanager/manager.go**: The `ManagerImpl` struct specifically manages device plugins and device allocation. It tracks device availability, health, allocation to pods, and interacts with the device plugin API to discover and manage resources exposed by device plugins. This is more specifically focused on device allocation and management compared to the generic plugin manager.\\n\\n## Component Relationships\\n- The `pod_workers` coordinates overall pod lifecycle by calling `SyncPod`\\n- `SyncPod` implementations delegate to `kubeGenericRuntimeManager.SyncPod()` for runtime operations\\n- The kuberuntime manager uses the CRI client (`remoteRuntimeService`) to communicate with container runtimes\\n- The volume manager runs independently to manage volume state\\n- The device managers coordinate to make device resources available to pods\\n\\nAll components follow the sig-node ownership pattern for kubelet functionality.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":4,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1781,"cache_read_input_tokens":54328,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1781},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"93196b35-4960-475b-ae0f-6a7fe42f974f","uuid":"c17464c7-ed0e-4fec-8ac3-fe23a0a7bfc2"}
